## �x�� NEUROMARKETING Y IA

### **Sistema de Neuromarketing Avanzado**
```python
import numpy as np
from scipy import signal
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class NeuromarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.eeg_processor = EEGProcessor()
        self.eye_tracker = EyeTracker()
        self.facial_coder = FacialCoder()
        self.galvanic_skin = GalvanicSkinResponse()
    
    def analyze_brain_response(self, eeg_data, stimulus):
        """Analizar respuesta cerebral a est��mulos"""
        # Procesar datos EEG
        processed_eeg = self.eeg_processor.process(eeg_data)
        
        # Extraer caracter��sticas relevantes
        features = {
            'alpha_power': self.extract_alpha_power(processed_eeg),
            'beta_power': self.extract_beta_power(processed_eeg),
            'theta_power': self.extract_theta_power(processed_eeg),
            'gamma_power': self.extract_gamma_power(processed_eeg),
            'attention_level': self.calculate_attention_level(processed_eeg),
            'emotional_arousal': self.calculate_emotional_arousal(processed_eeg)
        }
        
        return features
    
    def analyze_eye_movement(self, eye_tracking_data, visual_stimulus):
        """Analizar movimiento ocular"""
        eye_analysis = {
            'fixation_points': self.identify_fixation_points(eye_tracking_data),
            'saccade_patterns': self.analyze_saccade_patterns(eye_tracking_data),
            'heatmap': self.generate_heatmap(eye_tracking_data, visual_stimulus),
            'attention_areas': self.identify_attention_areas(eye_tracking_data),
            'reading_pattern': self.analyze_reading_pattern(eye_tracking_data)
        }
        
        return eye_analysis
    
    def analyze_facial_expressions(self, facial_data):
        """Analizar expresiones faciales"""
        expressions = {
            'emotions': self.detect_emotions(facial_data),
            'micro_expressions': self.detect_micro_expressions(facial_data),
            'valence': self.calculate_valence(facial_data),
            'arousal': self.calculate_arousal(facial_data),
            'dominance': self.calculate_dominance(facial_data)
        }
        
        return expressions
    
    def analyze_physiological_response(self, physiological_data):
        """Analizar respuesta fisiol��gica"""
        response = {
            'heart_rate': self.analyze_heart_rate(physiological_data.get('heart_rate')),
            'skin_conductance': self.analyze_skin_conductance(physiological_data.get('gsr')),
            'muscle_tension': self.analyze_muscle_tension(physiological_data.get('emg')),
            'respiration': self.analyze_respiration(physiological_data.get('respiration'))
        }
        
        return response
    
    def create_neuromarketing_insights(self, all_data):
        """Crear insights de neuromarketing"""
        insights = {
            'attention_score': self.calculate_attention_score(all_data),
            'emotional_impact': self.calculate_emotional_impact(all_data),
            'memory_encoding': self.assess_memory_encoding(all_data),
            'purchase_intent': self.predict_purchase_intent(all_data),
            'brand_recall': self.predict_brand_recall(all_data),
            'recommendations': self.generate_neuromarketing_recommendations(all_data)
        }
        
        return insights
    
    def optimize_marketing_content(self, neuromarketing_insights, content):
        """Optimizar contenido basado en neuromarketing"""
        optimized_content = {
            'visual_elements': self.optimize_visual_elements(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'text_content': self.optimize_text_content(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'layout': self.optimize_layout(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'colors': self.optimize_colors(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'timing': self.optimize_timing(neuromarketing_insights, content)
        }
        
        return optimized_content

class EEGProcessor:
    def process(self, eeg_data):
        """Procesar datos EEG"""
        # Filtrado de ruido
        filtered_data = self.filter_noise(eeg_data)
        
        # Extracci��n de caracter��sticas
        features = self.extract_features(filtered_data)
        
        return features
    
    def filter_noise(self, data):
        """Filtrar ruido de los datos EEG"""
        # Aplicar filtro de banda
        filtered = signal.butter(4, [1, 40], btype='band', fs=256, output='sos')
        filtered_data = signal.sosfilt(filtered, data)
        return filtered_data
    
    def extract_features(self, data):
        """Extraer caracter��sticas de los datos EEG"""
        features = {
            'power_spectral_density': self.calculate_psd(data),
            'coherence': self.calculate_coherence(data),
            'phase_locking': self.calculate_phase_locking(data)
        }
        return features

# Uso del neuromarketing
neuromarketing = NeuromarketingAI()
eeg_data = np.random.randn(256, 1000)  # Datos de ejemplo
brain_response = neuromarketing.analyze_brain_response(eeg_data, 'ad_stimulus')
```

## �xR� SOSTENIBILIDAD Y MARKETING VERDE CON IA

### **Sistema de Marketing Sostenible**
```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class SustainableMarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.carbon_footprint_calculator = CarbonFootprintCalculator()
        self.sustainability_metrics = SustainabilityMetrics()
        self.green_ai_optimizer = GreenAIOptimizer()
    
    def calculate_carbon_footprint(self, marketing_activities):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de actividades de marketing"""
        footprint = {
            'digital_ads': self.calculate_digital_ads_footprint(marketing_activities.get('digital_ads', [])),
            'email_campaigns': self.calculate_email_footprint(marketing_activities.get('emails', [])),
            'content_creation': self.calculate_content_footprint(marketing_activities.get('content', [])),
            'events': self.calculate_events_footprint(marketing_activities.get('events', [])),
            'packaging': self.calculate_packaging_footprint(marketing_activities.get('packaging', []))
        }
        
        total_footprint = sum(footprint.values())
        footprint['total'] = total_footprint
        footprint['equivalent'] = self.convert_to_equivalents(total_footprint)
        
        return footprint
    
    def calculate_digital_ads_footprint(self, digital_ads):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de anuncios digitales"""
        total_impressions = sum(ad.get('impressions', 0) for ad in digital_ads)
        total_clicks = sum(ad.get('clicks', 0) for ad in digital_ads)
        
        # Estimaci��n de CO2 por impresi��n y click
        co2_per_impression = 0.000001  # kg CO2
        co2_per_click = 0.00001  # kg CO2
        
        total_co2 = (total_impressions * co2_per_impression) + (total_clicks * co2_per_click)
        return total_co2
    
    def optimize_for_sustainability(self, marketing_strategy):
        """Optimizar estrategia de marketing para sostenibilidad"""
        optimized_strategy = {
            'channel_optimization': self.optimize_channels_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy),
            'content_optimization': self.optimize_content_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy),
            'timing_optimization': self.optimize_timing_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy),
            'targeting_optimization': self.optimize_targeting_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy)
        }
        
        return optimized_strategy
    
    def optimize_channels_for_sustainability(self, strategy):
        """Optimizar canales para sostenibilidad"""
        channel_sustainability = {
            'email': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000004, 'effectiveness': 0.8},
            'social_media': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000002, 'effectiveness': 0.6},
            'search_ads': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000001, 'effectiveness': 0.9},
            'display_ads': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000003, 'effectiveness': 0.4},
            'print_media': {'co2_per_contact': 0.01, 'effectiveness': 0.7}
        }
        
        # Seleccionar canales m��s sostenibles
        sustainable_channels = []
        for channel, metrics in channel_sustainability.items():
            sustainability_score = metrics['effectiveness'] / metrics['co2_per_contact']
            if sustainability_score > 1000:  # Umbral de sostenibilidad
                sustainable_channels.append({
                    'channel': channel,
                    'sustainability_score': sustainability_score,
                    'recommended_budget_share': self.calculate_budget_share(sustainability_score)
                })
        
        return sustainable_channels
    
    def create_sustainability_report(self, marketing_activities, period):
        """Crear reporte de sostenibilidad"""
        report = {
            'period': period,
            'carbon_footprint': self.calculate_carbon_footprint(marketing_activities),
            'sustainability_goals': self.assess_sustainability_goals(marketing_activities),
            'improvements': self.identify_improvements(marketing_activities),
            'recommendations': self.generate_sustainability_recommendations(marketing_activities),
            'benchmarks': self.compare_with_benchmarks(marketing_activities)
        }
        
        return report
    
    def assess_sustainability_goals(self, activities):
        """Evaluar objetivos de sostenibilidad"""
        goals = {
            'carbon_neutral': self.assess_carbon_neutrality(activities),
            'waste_reduction': self.assess_waste_reduction(activities),
            'renewable_energy': self.assess_renewable_energy_usage(activities),
            'circular_economy': self.assess_circular_economy_practices(activities)
        }
        
        return goals
    
    def generate_sustainability_recommendations(self, activities):
        """Generar recomendaciones de sostenibilidad"""
        recommendations = []
        
        # An��lisis de huella de carbono
        footprint = self.calculate_carbon_footprint(activities)
        if footprint['total'] > 1000:  # kg CO2
            recommendations.append({
                'priority': 'high',
                'category': 'carbon_reduction',
                'action': 'Implementar estrategias de marketing digital m��s eficientes',
                'potential_savings': '30-50% reducci��n en huella de carbono'
            })
        
        # An��lisis de canales
        channel_analysis = self.analyze_channel_sustainability(activities)
        if channel_analysis['least_sustainable']:
            recommendations.append({
                'priority': 'medium',
                'category': 'channel_optimization',
                'action': f"Reducir uso de {channel_analysis['least_sustainable']}",
                'potential_savings': '20-40% reducci��n en emisiones'
            })
        
        return recommendations

class CarbonFootprintCalculator:
    def __init__(self):
        self.emission_factors = {
            'electricity': 0.5,  # kg CO2 per kWh
            'data_center': 0.3,  # kg CO2 per GB
            'transportation': 0.2,  # kg CO2 per km
            'paper': 0.8  # kg CO2 per kg
        }
    
    def calculate_activity_footprint(self, activity_type, activity_data):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de una actividad espec��fica"""
        if activity_type == 'email_campaign':
            return self.calculate_email_footprint(activity_data)
        elif activity_type == 'digital_ad':
            return self.calculate_digital_ad_footprint(activity_data)
        elif activity_type == 'content_creation':
            return self.calculate_content_creation_footprint(activity_data)
        else:
            return 0
    
    def calculate_email_footprint(self, email_data):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de emails"""
        recipients = email_data.get('recipients', 0)
        email_size = email_data.get('size_mb', 0.1)
        
        # CO2 por email (aproximadamente 4g)
        co2_per_email = 0.004
        
        return recipients * co2_per_email

# Uso del marketing sostenible
sustainable_marketing = SustainableMarketingAI()
activities = {
    'digital_ads': [{'impressions': 1000000, 'clicks': 10000}],
    'emails': [{'recipients': 50000, 'size_mb': 0.1}],
    'content': [{'videos': 10, 'images': 50, 'articles': 20}]
}
footprint = sustainable_marketing.calculate_carbon_footprint(activities)
```

## �x}� M�0 TRICAS AVANZADAS DE �0 XITO

### **Dashboard de M��tricas Integrales**
```python
import plotly.graph_objects as go
from plotly.subplots import make_subplots
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

class AdvancedMetricsDashboard:
    def __init__(self):
        self.metrics = {}
        self.benchmarks = {}
        self.trends = {}
    
    def calculate_ai_marketing_roi(self, investment_data, revenue_data):
        """Calcular ROI de marketing con IA"""
        total_investment = sum(investment_data.values())
        total_revenue = sum(revenue_data.values())
        
        roi = ((total_revenue - total_investment) / total_investment) * 100
        
        return {
            'roi_percentage': roi,
            'total_investment': total_investment,
            'total_revenue': total_revenue,
            'net_profit': total_revenue - total_investment,
            'payback_period': self.calculate_payback_period(investment_data, revenue_data)
        }
    
    def calculate_customer_lifetime_value_ai(self, customer_data):
        """Calcular CLV con IA"""
        clv_metrics = {}
        
        for customer_id, data in customer_data.items():
            # Calcular CLV tradicional
            avg_order_value = data.get('avg_order_value', 0)
            purchase_frequency = data.get('purchase_frequency', 0)
            customer_lifespan = data.get('lifespan_months', 12)
            
            clv = avg_order_value * purchase_frequency * customer_lifespan
            
            # Ajustar con IA (predicci��n de comportamiento futuro)
            ai_multiplier = self.predict_ai_enhancement(customer_id, data)
            ai_enhanced_clv = clv * ai_multiplier
            
            clv_metrics[customer_id] = {
                'traditional_clv': clv,
                'ai_enhanced_clv': ai_enhanced_clv,
                'ai_multiplier': ai_multiplier,
                'improvement_percentage': ((ai_enhanced_clv - clv) / clv) * 100
            }
        
        return clv_metrics
    
    def calculate_ai_efficiency_metrics(self, before_ai, after_ai):
        """Calcular m��tricas de eficiencia de IA"""
        efficiency_metrics = {
            'time_savings': self.calculate_time_savings(before_ai, after_ai),
            'cost_reduction': self.calculate_cost_reduction(before_ai, after_ai),
            'accuracy_improvement': self.calculate_accuracy_improvement(before_ai, after_ai),
            'automation_rate': self.calculate_automation_rate(before_ai, after_ai),
            'scalability_factor': self.calculate_scalability_factor(before_ai, after_ai)
        }
        
        return efficiency_metrics
    
    def create_predictive_analytics_dashboard(self, historical_data, predictions):
        """Crear dashboard de analytics predictivos"""
        fig = make_subplots(
            rows=2, cols=2,
            subplot_titles=('Ventas Hist��ricas vs Predicciones', 'Tendencias de Conversi��n',
                          'An��lisis de Estacionalidad', 'ROI por Canal'),
            specs=[[{"secondary_y": True}, {"secondary_y": True}],
                   [{"secondary_y": True}, {"secondary_y": True}]]
        )
        
        # Gr��fico de ventas
        fig.add_trace(
            go.Scatter(x=historical_data['dates'], y=historical_data['sales'],
                      name='Ventas Hist��ricas', line=dict(color='blue')),
            row=1, col=1
        )
        
        fig.add_trace(
            go.Scatter(x=predictions['dates'], y=predictions['predicted_sales'],
                      name='Predicciones IA', line=dict(color='red', dash='dash')),
            row=1, col=1
        )
        
        # Gr��fico de conversi��n
        fig.add_trace(
            go.Scatter(x=historical_data['dates'], y=historical_data['conversion_rate'],
                      name='Tasa de Conversi��n', line=dict(color='green')),
            row=1, col=2
        )
        
        # Configurar layout
        fig.update_layout(
            title="Dashboard de Analytics Predictivos - IA Marketing",
            showlegend=True,
            height=800
        )
        
        return fig
    
    def calculate_ai_adoption_score(self, organization_data):
        """Calcular score de adopci��n de IA"""
        adoption_factors = {
            'tool_usage': organization_data.get('ai_tools_used', 0) / 10,
            'team_training': organization_data.get('team_ai_training', 0) / 100,
            'data_quality': organization_data.get('data_quality_score', 0) / 100,
            'process_automation': organization_data.get('automation_percentage', 0) / 100,
            'leadership_support': organization_data.get('leadership_support', 0) / 100
        }
        
        # Ponderar factores
        weights = {
            'tool_usage': 0.25,
            'team_training': 0.20,
            'data_quality': 0.25,
            'process_automation': 0.20,
            'leadership_support': 0.10
        }
        
        adoption_score = sum(adoption_factors[factor] * weights[factor] 
                           for factor in adoption_factors)
        
        return {
            'adoption_score': adoption_score * 100,
            'adoption_level': self.get_adoption_level(adoption_score),
            'improvement_areas': self.identify_improvement_areas(adoption_factors),
            'next_steps': self.recommend_next_steps(adoption_score)
        }
    
    def get_adoption_level(self, score):
        """Determinar nivel de adopci��n"""
        if score >= 0.8:
            return "L��der en IA"
        elif score >= 0.6:
            return "Avanzado"
        elif score >= 0.4:
            return "Intermedio"
        elif score >= 0.2:
            return "Principiante"
        else:
            return "Inicial"
    
    def identify_improvement_areas(self, adoption_factors):
        """Identificar ��reas de mejora"""
        improvement_areas = []
        
        for factor, score in adoption_factors.items():
            if score < 0.5:  # Umbral de mejora
                improvement_areas.append({
                    'area': factor,
                    'current_score': score * 100,
                    'priority': 'high' if score < 0.3 else 'medium',
                    'recommendations': self.get_improvement_recommendations(factor)
                })
        
        return improvement_areas

# Uso del dashboard avanzado
dashboard = AdvancedMetricsDashboard()
investment = {'ai_tools': 50000, 'training': 20000, 'infrastructure': 30000}
revenue = {'increased_sales': 200000, 'cost_savings': 50000, 'efficiency_gains': 30000}
roi = dashboard.calculate_ai_marketing_roi(investment, revenue)
```

`python
# Virtual Marketing Office
from marketing_ai import VirtualMarketingOffice

virtual_office = VirtualMarketingOffice(
    office_type="marketing_hub",
    capacity=100,
    features=["holographic_displays", "ai_creatives", "real_time_analytics"],
    timezone="global"
)

# ReuniÃ³n virtual de marketing
meeting = await virtual_office.schedule_marketing_meeting(
    campaign="Q1_Product_Launch",
    participants=["cmo", "creative_director", "data_analyst", "influencers"],
    duration="2_hours",
    format="immersive_brainstorming"
)

print(f"ðŸ‘¥ Participantes: {meeting.participants}")
print(f"â° DuraciÃ³n: {meeting.duration}")
print(f"ðŸŽ¯ Formato: {meeting.format}")
`

## 🤖 PROMPT ULTIMATE MEJORADO PARA SCRIBE - ASISTENTE DE IA MARKETING

### **Scribe - Especialista Senior en Marketing Digital con IA Avanzada**

Eres **Scribe**, un asistente de IA excepcional y especialista senior en marketing digital con vasto conocimiento en múltiples canales de marketing, estrategias de contenido, embudos de ventas y automatización avanzada.

### **Entorno: Marketing Lab Pro**

Operas en **Marketing Lab Pro**, una plataforma segura en el navegador que emula una suite completa de automatización de marketing empresarial. Todo el procesamiento y análisis de datos se ejecuta en el navegador con capacidades de IA integradas.

**Limitaciones del entorno:**
- **NO** puede ejecutar binarios nativos (solo código nativo del navegador: JS, WebAssembly, etc.)
- **Python limitado** a la biblioteca estándar únicamente (sin `pip`, sin librerías de terceros)
- **NO** hay compiladores C/C++ disponibles
- **Git NO** está disponible
- **NO** puede ejecutar edición diff/patch (siempre escribir código completo)

### **Operaciones de Base de Datos Avanzadas**

#### **Configuración por Defecto**
- **CRÍTICO**: Usar Supabase para bases de datos por defecto
- **IMPORTANTE**: La configuración del proyecto Supabase es manejada por el usuario
- **IMPORTANTE**: Crear archivo .env si no existe
- **NUNCA** modificar configuraciones de Supabase o archivos .env (excepto crear .env)
- **NO** generar tipos para Supabase

#### **Seguridad de Datos Avanzada**
- **CRÍTICO**: La integridad de datos es la máxima prioridad
- **PROHIBIDO**: Operaciones destructivas como `DROP` o `DELETE`
- **PROHIBIDO**: Declaraciones de control de transacciones
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Backup automático antes de cambios
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Validación de datos antes de inserción
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Logging de todas las operaciones

#### **Migraciones de Base de Datos Avanzadas**
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Proporcionar DOS acciones para cada cambio:
  1. **Creación de archivo de migración**
  2. **Ejecución inmediata de consulta**
- Crear archivos de migración en `/home/project/supabase/migrations`
- **NUNCA** actualizar archivos de migración existentes
- **SIEMPRE** habilitar RLS (Row Level Security) para nuevas tablas
- Incluir políticas RLS apropiadas para operaciones CRUD
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir rollback en cada migración
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Testing de migraciones antes de ejecución

#### **Estructura Avanzada de Archivos de Migración**
```sql
/*
# Resumen de Cambios
Descripción clara de los cambios en inglés simple
- Operaciones incluidas
- Políticas RLS implementadas
- Índices agregados
- Triggers creados
- Funciones definidas
- Rollback disponible
*/
-- Código SQL aquí
-- Rollback SQL aquí
```

### **Metodología de Trabajo Avanzada**

#### **Planificación Previa Inteligente**
Antes de proporcionar una solución, delinear BRIEFMENTE los pasos de implementación:
- Listar pasos concretos a seguir con estimaciones de tiempo
- Identificar componentes clave necesarios y dependencias
- Notar desafíos potenciales y soluciones alternativas
- Incluir métricas de éxito y KPIs
- Ser conciso (3-5 líneas máximo)

#### **Creación de Artefactos Avanzados**
Scribe crea un ÚNICO artefacto completo para cada proyecto que incluye:
- Comandos de shell a ejecutar (incluyendo dependencias NPM)
- Archivos a crear y su contenido completo
- Carpetas a crear si es necesario
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir documentación técnica
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir guías de usuario
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir tests y validaciones
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir métricas y KPIs

#### **Estructura Avanzada del Artefacto**
```xml
<boltArtifact title="Título del Proyecto" id="identificador-unico" version="1.0.0">
  <boltAction type="shell">comando-shell</boltAction>
  <boltAction type="file" path="ruta/archivo">contenido-completo</boltAction>
  <boltAction type="start">comando-inicio</boltAction>
  <boltAction type="test">comando-test</boltAction>
  <boltAction type="validate">comando-validacion</boltAction>
</boltArtifact>
```

#### **Reglas Críticas del Artefacto Avanzadas**
- **CRÍTICO**: Pensar HOLÍSTICAMENTE antes de crear el artefacto
- **IMPORTANTE**: Usar SIEMPRE las modificaciones más recientes de archivos
- **CRÍTICO**: Proporcionar SIEMPRE el contenido COMPLETO y actualizado
- **ALWAYS** instalar dependencias PRIMERO
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir validación y testing
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir documentación completa
- **IMPORTANTE**: Usar mejores prácticas de codificación y dividir funcionalidad en módulos más pequeños

### **Restricciones de Comunicación Avanzadas**
- **NUNCA** usar la palabra "artefacto"
- **IMPORTANTE**: Usar solo markdown válido (NO usar etiquetas HTML excepto en artefactos)
- **ULTRA IMPORTANTE**: NO ser verboso y NO explicar nada a menos que el usuario pida más información
- **ULTRA IMPORTANTE**: Pensar primero y responder con el artefacto que contiene todos los pasos necesarios para configurar el proyecto
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir métricas de éxito en cada respuesta
- **OBLIGATORIO**: Incluir estimaciones de tiempo de implementación

## �x}� MARKETING PREDICTIVO AVANZADO CON IA



### **Sistema de Predicci��n de Comportamiento del Cliente**

```python

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestRegressor, GradientBoostingRegressor

from sklearn.model_selection import TimeSeriesSplit

import xgboost as xgb

from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential

from tensorflow.keras.layers import LSTM, Dense, Dropout

import warnings

warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')



class PredictiveMarketingAI:

    def __init__(self):

        self.models = {}

        self.feature_importance = {}

        self.prediction_confidence = {}

    

    def create_customer_journey_predictor(self, customer_data, journey_stages):

        """Crear predictor de journey del cliente"""

        journey_predictor = {

            'awareness_prediction': self.predict_awareness_stage(customer_data),

            'consideration_prediction': self.predict_consideration_stage(customer_data),

            'purchase_prediction': self.predict_purchase_stage(customer_data),

            'retention_prediction': self.predict_retention_stage(customer_data),

            'advocacy_prediction': self.predict_advocacy_stage(customer_data)

        }

        

        return journey_predictor

    

    def predict_awareness_stage(self, customer_data):

        """Predecir etapa de awareness"""

        features = self.extract_awareness_features(customer_data)

        model = self.train_awareness_model(features)

        

        prediction = {

            'probability': model.predict_proba(features)[0][1],

            'confidence': self.calculate_confidence(model, features),

            'key_factors': self.identify_key_factors(model, features),

            'recommendations': self.generate_awareness_recommendations(features)

        }

        

        return prediction

    

    def predict_purchase_intent(self, customer_data, product_data):

        """Predecir intenci��n de compra"""

        # Combinar datos del cliente y producto

        combined_features = self.combine_customer_product_features(customer_data, product_data)

        

        # Entrenar modelo de intenci��n de compra

        model = self.train_purchase_intent_model(combined_features)

        

        # Hacer predicci��n

        intent_probability = model.predict_proba(combined_features)[0][1]

        

        # Calcular tiempo hasta compra

        time_to_purchase = self.predict_time_to_purchase(combined_features)

        

        # Generar recomendaciones

        recommendations = self.generate_purchase_recommendations(combined_features, intent_probability)

        

        return {

            'intent_probability': intent_probability,

            'time_to_purchase_days': time_to_purchase,

            'confidence': self.calculate_confidence(model, combined_features),

            'recommendations': recommendations,

            'key_drivers': self.identify_purchase_drivers(combined_features)

        }

    

    def predict_churn_risk(self, customer_data, historical_data):

        """Predecir riesgo de churn"""

        # Extraer caracter��sticas de riesgo

        risk_features = self.extract_churn_risk_features(customer_data, historical_data)

        

        # Entrenar modelo de churn

        model = self.train_churn_model(risk_features)

        

        # Calcular probabilidad de churn

        churn_probability = model.predict_proba(risk_features)[0][1]

        

        # Identificar factores de riesgo

        risk_factors = self.identify_churn_risk_factors(model, risk_features)

        

        # Generar estrategias de retenci��n

        retention_strategies = self.generate_retention_strategies(risk_factors, churn_probability)

        

        return {

            'churn_probability': churn_probability,

            'risk_level': self.categorize_risk_level(churn_probability),

            'risk_factors': risk_factors,

            'retention_strategies': retention_strategies,

            'intervention_urgency': self.calculate_intervention_urgency(churn_probability)

        }

    

    def predict_lifetime_value(self, customer_data, transaction_history):

        """Predecir valor de vida del cliente"""

        # Extraer caracter��sticas de CLV

        clv_features = self.extract_clv_features(customer_data, transaction_history)

        

        # Entrenar modelo de CLV

        model = self.train_clv_model(clv_features)

        

        # Predecir CLV

        predicted_clv = model.predict(clv_features)[0]

        

        # Calcular intervalos de confianza

        confidence_interval = self.calculate_clv_confidence_interval(model, clv_features)

        

        # Segmentar por valor

        value_segment = self.segment_by_value(predicted_clv)

        

        return {

            'predicted_clv': predicted_clv,

            'confidence_interval': confidence_interval,

            'value_segment': value_segment,

            'growth_potential': self.assess_growth_potential(clv_features),

            'retention_strategies': self.generate_clv_retention_strategies(value_segment)

        }

    

    def create_demand_forecasting_model(self, historical_sales, external_factors):

        """Crear modelo de pron��stico de demanda"""

        # Preparar datos de series temporales

        time_series_data = self.prepare_time_series_data(historical_sales, external_factors)

        

        # Entrenar modelo LSTM

        lstm_model = self.train_lstm_model(time_series_data)

        

        # Hacer pron��sticos

        forecasts = self.generate_forecasts(lstm_model, time_series_data, horizon=30)

        

        # Calcular intervalos de confianza

        confidence_intervals = self.calculate_forecast_confidence(lstm_model, time_series_data)

        

        # Identificar patrones estacionales

        seasonal_patterns = self.identify_seasonal_patterns(time_series_data)

        

        return {

            'forecasts': forecasts,

            'confidence_intervals': confidence_intervals,

            'seasonal_patterns': seasonal_patterns,

            'model_accuracy': self.evaluate_model_accuracy(lstm_model, time_series_data),

            'recommendations': self.generate_forecast_recommendations(forecasts)

        }

    

    def train_lstm_model(self, time_series_data):

        """Entrenar modelo LSTM para series temporales"""

        # Preparar datos para LSTM

        X, y = self.prepare_lstm_data(time_series_data)

        

        # Crear modelo LSTM

        model = Sequential([

            LSTM(50, return_sequences=True, input_shape=(X.shape[1], X.shape[2])),

            Dropout(0.2),

            LSTM(50, return_sequences=False),

            Dropout(0.2),

            Dense(25),

            Dense(1)

        ])

        

        # Compilar modelo

        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='mse', metrics=['mae'])

        

        # Entrenar modelo

        model.fit(X, y, epochs=100, batch_size=32, validation_split=0.2, verbose=0)

        

        return model

    

    def generate_marketing_insights(self, predictions):

        """Generar insights de marketing basados en predicciones"""

        insights = {

            'high_value_customers': self.identify_high_value_customers(predictions),

            'at_risk_customers': self.identify_at_risk_customers(predictions),

            'growth_opportunities': self.identify_growth_opportunities(predictions),

            'optimization_recommendations': self.generate_optimization_recommendations(predictions),

            'budget_allocation': self.recommend_budget_allocation(predictions)

        }

        

        return insights



# Uso del sistema predictivo

predictive_ai = PredictiveMarketingAI()

customer_data = {

    'demographics': {'age': 35, 'income': 75000, 'location': 'urban'},

    'behavior': {'page_views': 15, 'time_on_site': 300, 'email_opens': 3},

    'purchase_history': {'total_spent': 500, 'orders': 2, 'last_purchase': 30}

}

predictions = predictive_ai.create_customer_journey_predictor(customer_data, ['awareness', 'consideration', 'purchase'])

```

## �x�  AUTOMATIZACI� N INTELIGENTE DE MARKETING



### **Sistema de Automatizaci��n End-to-End**

```python

import schedule

import time

from datetime import datetime, timedelta

import smtplib

from email.mime.text import MIMEText

from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart

import requests

import json



class IntelligentMarketingAutomation:

    def __init__(self):

        self.workflows = {}

        self.triggers = {}

        self.actions = {}

        self.conditions = {}

        self.scheduled_tasks = {}

    

    def create_lead_nurturing_workflow(self, lead_data, nurturing_steps):

        """Crear workflow de nurturing de leads"""

        workflow = {

            'workflow_id': f"lead_nurturing_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}",

            'trigger': self.define_lead_trigger(lead_data),

            'steps': self.create_nurturing_steps(nurturing_steps),

            'conditions': self.define_nurturing_conditions(lead_data),

            'fallback_actions': self.define_fallback_actions()

        }

        

        self.workflows[workflow['workflow_id']] = workflow

        return workflow

    

    def create_nurturing_steps(self, steps_config):

        """Crear pasos de nurturing"""

        steps = []

        

        for i, step_config in enumerate(steps_config):

            step = {

                'step_id': f"step_{i+1}",

                'name': step_config.get('name', f'Step {i+1}'),

                'action': step_config.get('action'),

                'delay': step_config.get('delay_hours', 24),

                'conditions': step_config.get('conditions', []),

                'content': step_config.get('content'),

                'channel': step_config.get('channel', 'email')

            }

            steps.append(step)

        

        return steps

    

    def create_email_automation(self, email_config, recipient_list):

        """Crear automatizaci��n de emails"""

        email_automation = {

            'campaign_id': f"email_campaign_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}",

            'subject_line': email_config.get('subject'),

            'content': email_config.get('content'),

            'personalization': email_config.get('personalization', {}),

            'scheduling': email_config.get('scheduling', {}),

            'recipients': recipient_list,

            'tracking': email_config.get('tracking', True)

        }

        

        return email_automation

    

    def create_social_media_automation(self, platform, content_config):

        """Crear automatizaci��n de redes sociales"""

        social_automation = {

            'platform': platform,

            'content_type': content_config.get('type'),

            'content': content_config.get('content'),

            'scheduling': content_config.get('scheduling'),

            'hashtags': content_config.get('hashtags', []),

            'targeting': content_config.get('targeting', {}),

            'engagement_tracking': content_config.get('tracking', True)

        }

        

        return social_automation

    

    def create_abandoned_cart_recovery(self, cart_data, recovery_strategy):

        """Crear estrategia de recuperaci��n de carrito abandonado"""

        recovery_workflow = {

            'trigger': 'cart_abandoned',

            'timing': recovery_strategy.get('timing', [1, 24, 72]),  # horas

            'messages': self.create_recovery_messages(recovery_strategy),

            'incentives': recovery_strategy.get('incentives', []),

            'personalization': recovery_strategy.get('personalization', True)

        }

        

        return recovery_workflow

    

    def create_recovery_messages(self, strategy):

        """Crear mensajes de recuperaci��n"""

        messages = []

        

        for i, timing in enumerate(strategy.get('timing', [1, 24, 72])):

            message = {

                'sequence': i + 1,

                'delay_hours': timing,

                'subject': strategy.get('subjects', [])[i] if i < len(strategy.get('subjects', [])) else f"Don't forget your items!",

                'content': strategy.get('contents', [])[i] if i < len(strategy.get('contents', [])) else f"Complete your purchase now!",

                'cta': strategy.get('ctas', [])[i] if i < len(strategy.get('ctas', [])) else "Complete Purchase",

                'incentive': strategy.get('incentives', [])[i] if i < len(strategy.get('incentives', [])) else None

            }

            messages.append(message)

        

        return messages

    

    def create_dynamic_pricing_automation(self, product_data, pricing_rules):

        """Crear automatizaci��n de precios din��micos"""

        pricing_automation = {

            'product_id': product_data.get('id'),

            'base_price': product_data.get('price'),

            'rules': self.create_pricing_rules(pricing_rules),

            'triggers': self.define_pricing_triggers(pricing_rules),

            'adjustments': self.calculate_price_adjustments(product_data, pricing_rules),

            'monitoring': self.setup_pricing_monitoring()

        }

        

        return pricing_automation

    

    def create_pricing_rules(self, rules_config):

        """Crear reglas de precios"""

        rules = []

        

        for rule_config in rules_config:

            rule = {

                'rule_id': rule_config.get('id'),

                'condition': rule_config.get('condition'),

                'action': rule_config.get('action'),

                'value': rule_config.get('value'),

                'priority': rule_config.get('priority', 1),

                'active': rule_config.get('active', True)

            }

            rules.append(rule)

        

        return rules

    

    def create_customer_segmentation_automation(self, segmentation_rules):

        """Crear automatizaci��n de segmentaci��n de clientes"""

        segmentation_automation = {

            'rules': segmentation_rules,

            'update_frequency': 'daily',

            'segments': self.define_customer_segments(segmentation_rules),

            'actions': self.define_segment_actions(segmentation_rules),

            'monitoring': self.setup_segmentation_monitoring()

        }

        

        return segmentation_automation

    

    def define_customer_segments(self, rules):

        """Definir segmentos de clientes"""

        segments = {

            'high_value': {

                'criteria': rules.get('high_value_criteria', {}),

                'description': 'High-value customers with high CLV',

                'action': 'premium_campaign'

            },

            'at_risk': {

                'criteria': rules.get('at_risk_criteria', {}),

                'description': 'Customers at risk of churning',

                'action': 'retention_campaign'

            },

            'new_customers': {

                'criteria': rules.get('new_customer_criteria', {}),

                'description': 'Recently acquired customers',

                'action': 'onboarding_campaign'

            },

            'loyal_customers': {

                'criteria': rules.get('loyal_customer_criteria', {}),

                'description': 'Long-term loyal customers',

                'action': 'loyalty_campaign'

            }

        }

        

        return segments

    

    def create_cross_channel_automation(self, channels, coordination_rules):

        """Crear automatizaci��n cross-channel"""

        cross_channel_automation = {

            'channels': channels,

            'coordination_rules': coordination_rules,

            'message_consistency': self.ensure_message_consistency(channels),

            'timing_coordination': self.coordinate_timing(channels),

            'personalization': self.coordinate_personalization(channels),

            'tracking': self.setup_cross_channel_tracking(channels)

        }

        

        return cross_channel_automation

    

    def execute_automation_workflow(self, workflow_id, trigger_data):

        """Ejecutar workflow de automatizaci��n"""

        workflow = self.workflows.get(workflow_id)

        if not workflow:

            return {'error': 'Workflow not found'}

        

        execution_log = {

            'workflow_id': workflow_id,

            'start_time': datetime.now(),

            'trigger_data': trigger_data,

            'steps_executed': [],

            'results': []

        }

        

        # Ejecutar cada paso del workflow

        for step in workflow['steps']:

            step_result = self.execute_workflow_step(step, trigger_data)

            execution_log['steps_executed'].append(step['step_id'])

            execution_log['results'].append(step_result)

        

        execution_log['end_time'] = datetime.now()

        execution_log['status'] = 'completed'

        

        return execution_log

    

    def execute_workflow_step(self, step, trigger_data):

        """Ejecutar paso individual del workflow"""

        step_result = {

            'step_id': step['step_id'],

            'action': step['action'],

            'status': 'pending',

            'timestamp': datetime.now()

        }

        

        try:

            if step['action'] == 'send_email':

                result = self.send_automated_email(step, trigger_data)

            elif step['action'] == 'update_segment':

                result = self.update_customer_segment(step, trigger_data)

            elif step['action'] == 'create_task':

                result = self.create_follow_up_task(step, trigger_data)

            elif step['action'] == 'send_notification':

                result = self.send_notification(step, trigger_data)

            else:

                result = {'status': 'unknown_action'}

            

            step_result['status'] = 'completed'

            step_result['result'] = result

            

        except Exception as e:

            step_result['status'] = 'failed'

            step_result['error'] = str(e)

        

        return step_result



# Uso del sistema de automatizaci��n

automation = IntelligentMarketingAutomation()

lead_data = {

    'source': 'website',

    'score': 85,

    'industry': 'technology',

    'company_size': 'medium'

}

nurturing_steps = [

    {'name': 'Welcome Email', 'action': 'send_email', 'delay_hours': 1},

    {'name': 'Educational Content', 'action': 'send_email', 'delay_hours': 24},

    {'name': 'Product Demo', 'action': 'create_task', 'delay_hours': 72}

]

workflow = automation.create_lead_nurturing_workflow(lead_data, nurturing_steps)

```

```python
import plotly.graph_objects as go

from plotly.subplots import make_subplots

import plotly.express as px

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from sklearn.metrics import mean_absolute_error, mean_squared_error, r2_score

import seaborn as sns

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt



class AdvancedAnalyticsAI:

    def __init__(self):

        self.models = {}

        self.metrics = {}

        self.visualizations = {}

        self.insights = {}

    

    def create_predictive_dashboard(self, data, predictions, metrics):

        """Crear dashboard predictivo interactivo"""

        fig = make_subplots(

            rows=3, cols=2,

            subplot_titles=('Ventas Reales vs Predicciones', 'Tendencias de Conversi��n',

                          'An��lisis de Segmentos', 'ROI por Canal',

                          'An��lisis de Estacionalidad', 'M��tricas de Rendimiento'),

            specs=[[{"secondary_y": True}, {"secondary_y": True}],

                   [{"secondary_y": True}, {"secondary_y": True}],

                   [{"secondary_y": True}, {"secondary_y": True}]]

        )

        

        # Gr��fico 1: Ventas Reales vs Predicciones

        fig.add_trace(

            go.Scatter(x=data['dates'], y=data['actual_sales'],

                      name='Ventas Reales', line=dict(color='blue')),

            row=1, col=1

        )

        fig.add_trace(

            go.Scatter(x=data['dates'], y=predictions['predicted_sales'],

                      name='Predicciones IA', line=dict(color='red', dash='dash')),

            row=1, col=1

        )

        

        # Gr��fico 2: Tendencias de Conversi��n

        fig.add_trace(

            go.Scatter(x=data['dates'], y=data['conversion_rate'],

                      name='Tasa de Conversi��n', line=dict(color='green')),

            row=1, col=2

        )

        

        # Gr��fico 3: An��lisis de Segmentos

        segment_data = self.analyze_customer_segments(data)

        fig.add_trace(

            go.Bar(x=segment_data['segments'], y=segment_data['values'],

                  name='Valor por Segmento'),

            row=2, col=1

        )

        

        # Gr��fico 4: ROI por Canal

        roi_data = self.calculate_roi_by_channel(data)

        fig.add_trace(

            go.Bar(x=roi_data['channels'], y=roi_data['roi'],

                  name='ROI por Canal'),

            row=2, col=2

        )

        

        # Gr��fico 5: An��lisis de Estacionalidad

        seasonal_data = self.analyze_seasonality(data)

        fig.add_trace(

            go.Scatter(x=seasonal_data['months'], y=seasonal_data['pattern'],

                      name='Patr��n Estacional'),

            row=3, col=1

        )

        

        # Gr��fico 6: M��tricas de Rendimiento

        performance_data = self.calculate_performance_metrics(metrics)

        fig.add_trace(

            go.Indicator(

                mode="gauge+number+delta",

                value=performance_data['overall_score'],

                domain={'x': [0, 1], 'y': [0, 1]},

                title={'text': "Score General"},

                delta={'reference': performance_data['previous_score']},

                gauge={'axis': {'range': [None, 100]},

                       'bar': {'color': "darkblue"},

                       'steps': [{'range': [0, 50], 'color': "lightgray"},

                                {'range': [50, 80], 'color': "gray"}],

                       'threshold': {'line': {'color': "red", 'width': 4},

                                   'thickness': 0.75, 'value': 90}}

            ),

            row=3, col=2

        )

        

        # Configurar layout

        fig.update_layout(

            title="Dashboard de Analytics Predictivos - IA Marketing",

            showlegend=True,

            height=1200,

            width=1400

        )

        

        return fig

    

    def create_attribution_analysis(self, touchpoint_data, conversion_data):

        """Crear an��lisis de atribuci��n"""

        attribution_analysis = {

            'first_touch': self.calculate_first_touch_attribution(touchpoint_data, conversion_data),

            'last_touch': self.calculate_last_touch_attribution(touchpoint_data, conversion_data),

            'linear': self.calculate_linear_attribution(touchpoint_data, conversion_data),

            'time_decay': self.calculate_time_decay_attribution(touchpoint_data, conversion_data),

            'position_based': self.calculate_position_based_attribution(touchpoint_data, conversion_data),

            'data_driven': self.calculate_data_driven_attribution(touchpoint_data, conversion_data)

        }

        

        return attribution_analysis

    

    def calculate_first_touch_attribution(self, touchpoints, conversions):

        """Calcular atribuci��n de primer toque"""

        first_touch_attribution = {}

        

        for conversion in conversions:

            customer_id = conversion['customer_id']

            customer_touchpoints = touchpoints[touchpoints['customer_id'] == customer_id]

            

            if not customer_touchpoints.empty:

                first_touchpoint = customer_touchpoints.iloc[0]

                channel = first_touchpoint['channel']

                

                if channel not in first_touch_attribution:

                    first_touch_attribution[channel] = 0

                first_touch_attribution[channel] += conversion['value']

        

        return first_touch_attribution

    

    def calculate_data_driven_attribution(self, touchpoints, conversions):

        """Calcular atribuci��n basada en datos"""

        # Implementar algoritmo de atribuci��n basado en datos

        # Usando machine learning para determinar el valor de cada touchpoint

        

        from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestRegressor

        from sklearn.preprocessing import LabelEncoder

        

        # Preparar datos para ML

        features = self.prepare_attribution_features(touchpoints, conversions)

        

        # Entrenar modelo

        model = RandomForestRegressor(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)

        model.fit(features['X'], features['y'])

        

        # Calcular importancia de features (touchpoints)

        feature_importance = model.feature_importances_

        channel_importance = dict(zip(features['channels'], feature_importance))

        

        return channel_importance

    

    def create_cohort_analysis(self, customer_data, cohort_period='month'):

        """Crear an��lisis de cohortes"""

        cohort_data = self.prepare_cohort_data(customer_data, cohort_period)

        

        # Calcular retenci��n por cohorte

        retention_matrix = self.calculate_retention_matrix(cohort_data)

        

        # Calcular m��tricas de cohorte

        cohort_metrics = {

            'retention_rates': retention_matrix,

            'average_retention': self.calculate_average_retention(retention_matrix),

            'cohort_sizes': self.calculate_cohort_sizes(cohort_data),

            'revenue_by_cohort': self.calculate_revenue_by_cohort(cohort_data),

            'lifetime_value_by_cohort': self.calculate_ltv_by_cohort(cohort_data)

        }

        

        return cohort_metrics

    

    def create_funnel_analysis(self, funnel_data):

        """Crear an��lisis de embudo"""

        funnel_analysis = {

            'stages': self.identify_funnel_stages(funnel_data),

            'conversion_rates': self.calculate_conversion_rates(funnel_data),

            'drop_off_points': self.identify_drop_off_points(funnel_data),

            'optimization_opportunities': self.identify_optimization_opportunities(funnel_data),

            'benchmarks': self.compare_with_benchmarks(funnel_data)

        }

        

        return funnel_analysis

    

    def create_advanced_segmentation(self, customer_data, segmentation_method='kmeans'):

        """Crear segmentaci��n avanzada"""

        if segmentation_method == 'kmeans':

            segments = self.kmeans_segmentation(customer_data)

        elif segmentation_method == 'rfm':

            segments = self.rfm_segmentation(customer_data)

        elif segmentation_method == 'behavioral':

            segments = self.behavioral_segmentation(customer_data)

        else:

            segments = self.hybrid_segmentation(customer_data)

        

        return segments

    

    def kmeans_segmentation(self, customer_data):

        """Segmentaci��n con K-means"""

        from sklearn.cluster import KMeans

        from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler

        

        # Preparar datos

        features = self.prepare_segmentation_features(customer_data)

        scaler = StandardScaler()

        features_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(features)

        

        # Determinar n��mero ��ptimo de clusters

        optimal_k = self.find_optimal_k(features_scaled)

        

        # Aplicar K-means

        kmeans = KMeans(n_clusters=optimal_k, random_state=42)

        clusters = kmeans.fit_predict(features_scaled)

        

        # Analizar clusters

        segment_analysis = self.analyze_segments(features, clusters)

        

        return segment_analysis

    

    def create_anomaly_detection(self, data, anomaly_threshold=0.05):

        """Crear detecci��n de anomal��as"""

        from sklearn.ensemble import IsolationForest

        from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler

        

        # Preparar datos

        features = self.prepare_anomaly_features(data)

        scaler = StandardScaler()

        features_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(features)

        

        # Aplicar Isolation Forest

        isolation_forest = IsolationForest(contamination=anomaly_threshold, random_state=42)

        anomaly_labels = isolation_forest.fit_predict(features_scaled)

        

        # Identificar anomal��as

        anomalies = data[anomaly_labels == -1]

        

        # Analizar anomal��as

        anomaly_analysis = {

            'anomalies_detected': len(anomalies),

            'anomaly_rate': len(anomalies) / len(data),

            'anomaly_types': self.categorize_anomalies(anomalies),

            'recommendations': self.generate_anomaly_recommendations(anomalies)

        }

        

        return anomaly_analysis

    

    def create_advanced_forecasting(self, time_series_data, forecast_horizon=30):

        """Crear pron��sticos avanzados"""

        from statsmodels.tsa.arima.model import ARIMA

        from statsmodels.tsa.seasonal import seasonal_decompose

        from statsmodels.tsa.holtwinters import ExponentialSmoothing

        

        # Descomposici��n estacional

        decomposition = seasonal_decompose(time_series_data, model='additive')

        

        # Modelo ARIMA

        arima_model = ARIMA(time_series_data, order=(1, 1, 1))

        arima_fit = arima_model.fit()

        arima_forecast = arima_fit.forecast(steps=forecast_horizon)

        

        # Modelo de suavizado exponencial

        exp_smoothing = ExponentialSmoothing(time_series_data, trend='add', seasonal='add')

        exp_fit = exp_smoothing.fit()

        exp_forecast = exp_fit.forecast(steps=forecast_horizon)

        

        # Combinar pron��sticos

        combined_forecast = self.combine_forecasts(arima_forecast, exp_forecast)

        

        # Calcular intervalos de confianza

        confidence_intervals = self.calculate_forecast_confidence(combined_forecast)

        

        return {

            'forecast': combined_forecast,

            'confidence_intervals': confidence_intervals,

            'model_accuracy': self.evaluate_forecast_accuracy(arima_fit, exp_fit),

            'seasonal_patterns': decomposition.seasonal,

            'trend': decomposition.trend,

            'residuals': decomposition.resid

        }



# Uso del sistema de analytics avanzados

analytics = AdvancedAnalyticsAI()

    'dates': pd.date_range('2024-01-01', periods=365),

    'actual_sales': np.random.randn(365).cumsum() + 1000,

    'conversion_rate': np.random.uniform(0.02, 0.08, 365)

}

predictions = {

    'predicted_sales': np.random.randn(365).cumsum() + 1000

}

metrics = {

    'mae': 50.2,

    'rmse': 75.8,

    'r2': 0.85

}

dashboard = analytics.create_predictive_dashboard(data, predictions, metrics)

```
